{"kind": "blogger#postList", "nextPageToken": "CgkIChjAwOHo8yQQy4Ca9ZL8nrwx", "items": [{"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "8515761173777426842", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-04-30T09:38:00+05:30", "updated": "2018-08-02T08:48:04+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNTMzMTc5ODg0MDUwCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/04/dynamic-risk-assessment-on-chemical.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/8515761173777426842", "title": "DYNAMIC RISK ASSESSMENT ON CHEMICAL TANKERS-- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S9pZkmfXufI/AAAAAAAAANI/GLrA9gQZJ6c/s1600/ra.jpg\"><img alt=\"\" border=\"0\" id=\"BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5465779583109806578\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S9pZkmfXufI/AAAAAAAAANI/GLrA9gQZJ6c/s320/ra.jpg\" style=\"cursor: pointer; float: left; height: 84px; margin: 0px 10px 10px 0px; width: 134px;\" /></a><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nDYNAMIC RISK ASSESSMENT matrix must consider <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">SEVERITY , CERTAINTY </span>and <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">PERIOD OF IMPACT.</span><br />\n<br />\nThe whole world ignores PERIOD OF IMPACT. On risk prone parcel chemical tankers we do not have the luxury of ignoring this crucial factor. On stubbing your toe, you will get most \" severe pain\"  , \" certainly\"  for 3 seconds. Nobody minds this short period pain. However LONG period of such pain is not an option.<br />\n<br />\nIn a nutshell , DRA is the CONTINOUS ASSESSMENT of risk in a rapidly changing environment like a ship on fire, chemical tanker having toxic spill, or collision/ grounding.  Or  analyzing new control measures when the changing degree of risk demands it ( suddenly reserve buoyancy at risk --or as the fire spreads,  new toxic gases are released ).<br />\n<br />\nCommonsense and experience dictates that no risk assessment can be static \u2013 it has to be dynamic, as the events unfold.  Focus on any emergency response must change as the incident evolves.<br />\n<br />\nThere is something as a \u2013<br />\nInitial stage<br />\nDevelopment stage<br />\nand <br />\na closing stage.<br />\n<br />\nIn the development stage, safe systems of response have indeed been initially selected and assessed, additional control measures introduced and an optimum course of action chalked out.<br />\n<br />\nA good  emergency response system must assign a competent person to do the process of --    \u201c MEASUREMENT \u201c -- in a mundane PLAN/ ACT/ MEASURE/ IMPROVE cycle. <br />\n<br />\nThis \u201cmeasurement squad\u201d , boils down to a \u201croving squad\u201d consisting of a think tank ( usually Chief engineer and Electrical officer ) who are the ears and eyes of a Master who is blind and deaf on the bridge\u2014yet , has to take critical decisions.  He is short of  feedback from a clear / experienced / competent brain who is observing from dynamic vantage positions \u2014in the lookout for coming shadows and thinking of ways to avoid secondary dangers, all the time reviewing the effectiveness of the existing control measures.. <br />\n<br />\nIn the old system ( discarded whole sale by the entire Annex 1 and Annex 2 tanker industry 15 years back )  the chief engineer was relegated to maintaining essential services and doing normal watchkeeping in the engine room , where he is not as familiar with valves and pipelines as the usual EOW.<br />\n<br />\nWe had a situation where both the 4 stripers were deaf and blind,  the 3 stripers are busy doing something, and nobody watching the larger DYNAMIC picture unfolding.  On the contrary a 4 striper  should be all over the place , including the engine room ( when warranted ) and on bridge to hold critical intelligence information exchanges on new tactical modes/ stopping something happening the wrong way , (based on DRA) with the Master .<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-h2KrV1AzFZI/TmAUgS2AXQI/AAAAAAAAF4w/5mAMMy_jYSI/s1600/imagesCA6ZURW9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-h2KrV1AzFZI/TmAUgS2AXQI/AAAAAAAAF4w/5mAMMy_jYSI/s1600/imagesCA6ZURW9.jpg\" /></a></div>\n&nbsp; <br />\nIt  must be appreciated that everything cannot be told on the walkie talkie in an emergency\u2014including a TRUE report on how the Chief Officer ( on OFFENSIVE TACTICAL MODE ) and Second Engineer ( on DEFENSIVE TACTICAL MODE )  is managing their teams \u2013for engine emergencies vice versa.<br />\n<br />\nIn other words the ROVING SQUAD TAKES CARE OF THE TRANSITIONAL MODE including :---<br />\nmonitoring the physical conditions of the offensive and defensive leaders,<br />\nevaluating competence of allocated tasks , <br />\nevaluating the larger picture ( life/ property/ pollution/ image )<br />\nevaluating if the calculated risk taken outweighs the benefits.<br />\n--and if indeed so , if there are any viable alternatives.<br />\n<br />\nHe is now able to tender specialist advise to the blind and deaf decision maker on the bridge ( read that as Master ) <br />\n<br />\n+TRANSITIONAL ( THE CRACK FILLER ) = OFFENSIVE  (+ )DEFENSIVE <br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTHE PROCESS--<br />\n<br />\nA seaman sees a huge round stone overhanging a ledge on the ship on top of a passage way used by the whole crew. He identifies this as a HAZARD. <br />\n<br />\nNow what is a hazard?<br />\n<br />\nA hazard is something which is of potential danger , but it has NOT YET HAPPENED . This can be compared to a fishing boat right ahead while sailing. The look out man who reports this to the OOW has reported a HAZARD. <br />\n<br />\nON PRO-ACTIVE CULTURED CHEMICAL TANKERS WE LIKE TO HEAR OF HAZARD WHICH HAVE NOT YET HAPPENED \u2013THE SAME WAY THE BRIDGE OOW WILL TAKE A DIM VIEW OF THE LOOKOUT MAN WHO REPORTS FISHING BOATS IN THE SHIPS WAKE.<br />\n<br />\nOnce the fishing boat has gone behind the ships wake , it is no longer a hazard, for it has happened. It could now be classified as a NEAR MISS if the ship missed it narrowly or it just grazed the ship\u2014scrapping off paint and causing a scratch.<br />\n<br />\nOf course if the fishing boat was damaged severely or it sank it is now classified as an ACCIDENT.<br />\n<br />\nNow let us get back to good old stone. The seaman has  reported the stone , which is a source of potential harm,  to the chief officer. <br />\n<br />\nIt is now the ships managements duty to do RISK ASSESSMENT and then do RISK MANAGEMENT.<br />\n<br />\nRISK ASSESSMENT since it includes the consequences  has 6 DYNAMIC aspects:--<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">Severity\u2014minor loss ( injury ) to total loss ( death )  </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">Time of impact /Recovery ---  rapid recovery to irreversible ( first aid to full life in wheelchair  / long term impact to environment )</span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Frequency--- remote to occasional to progressively increasing.( this is more related to security than safety-- if a car is driven daily it will have less chance of a breakdown than a car which is take out once in 2 years. But if you sail close to Somalian coast daily your chances of getting pirated is higher than if you sail once in 2 years )&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">Certainty--- 100% sure ? YES or NO </span><br />\n<br />\nImage\u2014loss of image is abstract and is about loss of business ( cannot trade in USA, loss of oil major long term time  charters etc ).<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nThe ships management holds a risk assessment meeting and now decides to do RISK MANAGEMENT based on the well known T4 principles\u2014<br />\n<br />\n1) Terminate/ throw the nil value stone overboard ( eliminate,  amputate )<br />\n<br />\n2) Treat/ Lash up the stone with wires and wedges ( safeguards like extinguishers, reduce risk to acceptable level )<br />\n<br />\n3) Tolerate/ Isolate and manage ( close the passage or use a deflector so that it falls elsewhere, PPE )<br />\n<br />\n4) Transfer/ Call for special and skilled help or advise.  ( call a shore workshop )<br />\n<br />\nWhat T to use-- is determined by weighing if the RESIDUAL risk outweighs the benefits.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">Risk Matrix</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">RISK = POTENTIAL SEVERITY x IMPACT PERIOD X CERTAINTY ( AS A YES/ NO SWITCH )</span><br />\n<br />\nTABLE 1, 2 AND 3 TO BE CHECKED,  IF IN TABLE 3 ITEM \u201c YES\u201d  IS APPLICABLE.  <br />\n<br />\nTHEN IN TABLE 4 , ITEM  WILL BE  ONE STEP HIGHER ( HIGH BECOMES UNACCEPTABLE,<br />\nMEDIUM GOES TO HIGH   , LOW GOES TO MEDIUM )<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">TABLE 1 \u2013 POTENTIAL SEVERITY</span><br />\n<br />\nSeverity Category/ Health and Safety Impact/ Damage to Vessel-Property/ Environmental Impact/ Contamination of next cargo<br />\n<br />\nV Fatal Accident Total Loss/   Major Impact to Environment <br />\n(Liquids -- spill/discharge in water &gt; 1m3)/ Highly Contaminated/  Readily Apparent and vessel cannot pass  manifold sample<br />\n<br />\nIV Serious Accident with possible Permanent Injury Damage requiring external assistance/ Significant Impact to Environment (Liquids -- Spill/discharge in water &gt; 150L and &lt; 1m3)/ Vessel Cannot pass first foot sample/  III Serious Personal Injury Damage which can be repaired by crew/ Impact to Environment .(Liquids --Spill/discharge in water &gt; 10L and &lt; 150L)/ Possible Contamination of minor nature  II Injury requiring Medical Treatment/  Minor damage/ Minor Impact to Environment (Liquids -- Spill/discharge in water &gt; 1L and &lt; 10L)/ Possible Contamination of insignificant nature  I First Aid Injury/ Insignificant damage/ Little Impact to Environment (Liquids -- Spill/discharge in water &lt; 1L)/ Contamination not affecting next cargo&nbsp;   <br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">TABLE 2 \u2013  IMPACT PERIOD DIRECT AND INDIRECT </span> Risk Letter/ Effect Time period  A IRREVERSIBLE loss of company image and business PERMANENT B Major impact for very long time &gt; 5 Years<br />\nC Moderate impact for long time &gt;6 months \u2013 1 year<br />\nD Some Impact for some time &gt;1 day <br />\nE Minor impact for very short time &lt; 1 Hour  <br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">TABLE 3 -- CERTAINTY</span><br />\n<br />\nRisk Letter Certainty of Happening<br />\nY -100 % SURE<br />\nN - Possible<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: cyan;\">TABLE 4  -- RISK MATRIX&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\nIn cases where the Determined Risk is:<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Un Acceptable</span> :  ABORT!  Await shore senior management level decision<br />\n(Higher premiums to be  paid)<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: white;\">High</span>:</span> Work shall NOT start. Appropriate additional controls taken to reduce<br />\nresidual high risk level to Moderate or Low<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Moderate</span>: Efforts  made to reduce the risk, with monitoring of the additional <br />\ncontrols that are implemented<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">Low</span>: No additional controls required, monitoring required to ensure existing <br />\ncontrols are maintained<br />\n<br />\nA B C D E  <br />\nV U H H H M  <br />\nIV H H H M M  <br />\nIII H H M M L  <br />\nII H M M L L  <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; float: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n<img src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-0Gvy5mBcipE/WlAJZNfU3zI/AAAAAAABXsU/wZaBJr4cOoclmnshY0dz6Y3NbokDpLaaACK4BGAYYCw/s35/*\" style=\"border: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); max-width: 36px;\" /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c3153449960981984161\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_0M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "12", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/8515761173777426842/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "8083689494400841863", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-04-30T09:12:00+05:30", "updated": "2019-03-16T18:20:25+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxNTUyNzQwNjI1NzAyCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/04/deionised-or-demineralised-water.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/8083689494400841863", "title": "DEIONISED  OR  DEMINERALISED  WATER  -- CHEMICAL TANKERS--  CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-R3FhW3XUDWU/XIzvZxD7z-I/AAAAAAABgLQ/c-ybXDmCFT0_OkIIsw1ZuNe5jqAYyr20ACLcBGAs/s1600/priffmer_T_Ion_Exchange_CHromatography.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"326\" data-original-width=\"465\" height=\"448\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-R3FhW3XUDWU/XIzvZxD7z-I/AAAAAAABgLQ/c-ybXDmCFT0_OkIIsw1ZuNe5jqAYyr20ACLcBGAs/s640/priffmer_T_Ion_Exchange_CHromatography.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ycwyKdnGABY/XIzvzPlgq8I/AAAAAAABgLY/FpA8hU4zmKY1PrFLeWwZAovjdBiMZuXtACLcBGAs/s1600/Fwwig58.PNG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"253\" data-original-width=\"580\" height=\"278\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-ycwyKdnGABY/XIzvzPlgq8I/AAAAAAABgLY/FpA8hU4zmKY1PrFLeWwZAovjdBiMZuXtACLcBGAs/s640/Fwwig58.PNG\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nDI WATER/ DEMI WATER -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nDI water is used to flush out the chlorides from CHEMICAL TANKER tank bulkheads prior sensitive wall wash cargoes . <br />\n<br />\n###########<br />\nMethanol cannot dissolve chlorides. Water is a good solvent for salt . It has a high di-electric constant or relative permitivity. ( 81 --it has no units ). This means the force of attraction between ions is 81 times less in water than in a vacuum and this allows them to separate. High di-electric constant is equivalent to high insulating properties to lower the attraction between the oppositely charged ions once they are solvated. Water solvates both cations and anions.  When you do a chloride wall wash test rememer that a pinch of salt put in methanol remains there , and water is the best solvent.<br />\n<br />\nBASICS: A positive ion is called a cation and negative ion is called anion.  The protons and neutrons are held together very tightly in the nuclues. But the outer orbital electrons are held very loosely. They can jump from one atom to another. It is also possible to shift electrons from one atom to another.  The atom which loses one electron has  one excess proton as a result in the tight nucleus and thus gets unbalanced. Such an atom is called a positive ion. <br />\n##########<br />\n<br />\nIon exchange units are insoluble, cross linked, long chain organic polymers with microporous structure and the functional groups attached to the chain are responsible for ion exchanging properties. <br />\n<br />\nResins containing acidic functional groups are capable of exchanging H+ ions with other cations.<br />\n<br />\nResins containing basic functional groups are capable of exchanging anions with other anions.<br />\n<br />\nIon Exchangers are thus insoluble granular substances which have in their molecular structure acidic or basic radicals that can exchange. The positive or negative ions fixed on these radicals are replaced by ions of the same sign in solution in the liquid in contact with them.<br />\n<br />\nCATION EXCHANGE RESINS:   Copolymers which on sulphonation and carboxylation become capable to exchange their hydrogen ions / H+ with cations in water. <br />\n<br />\nANION EXCHANGE RESINS:   Copolymers which after treating with NAOH solution become capable to exchange their OH- ions with anions in water.<br />\n<br />\nFirst filter the water to reduce turbidity to less than 10 ppm.<br />\n<br />\nThen this filtered water is first passed through cation exchange cylinder which removes CA2+/ MG2+ ( water hardness ions ) cations from it and an equivalent amount of H+ ions are released into the water. The water is now softened. &nbsp;(THIS ACIDIC WATER CAN DESTROY YOUR ZINC SILICATE COATING WHICH CANNOT TAKE pH LESS THAN 6.)<br />\n<br />\nThen this water is passed through an anion exchange cylinder which removes  SO42-  CL-  ( chlorides ) anions from it and an equivalent amount  of OH- ions are released into the water. The chlorides are now removed. The water is now called de ionized water or de mineralized water.<br />\n<br />\nThe ion exchange is complete without deterioration or changing the total number of ions in the liquid before the exchange <br />\n<br />\nH+ cations and OH- anions get combined to form a water molecule H2O. <br />\n<br />\nWhen the capacity of cation and anion exchangers to exchange H+ and OH- ions is lost they are said to be exhausted.  Regeneration of cation cylinder is done by dilute Hydrochloric acid or Sulphuric acid .<br />\n<br />\nAnion cylinder is regenerated by dilute Sodium Hydroxide. Then both the cylinders are washed with DI water to wash of the unwanted Ca2+, Mg2+, SO42, CL- ions. <br />\n<br />\nRegardless of brand, the core principles of ion exhange resin remain the same. There are 4 main types of resin, each with their own function:  Strong acid cation (SAC), Weak acid cation (WAC) , Strong base anion (SBA), Weak base anion (WBA).<br />\n<br />\nMIXED BED :<br />\nMixed Bed resins, sometimes referred to as mix bed resin, are a combination of cation and anion resins. Usually the ratio for mixed bed resin is 1:1 or 1:2 depending on the application.<br />\n<br />\nSingle cylinder containing intimate mixture of cation/ anion exchange resins. When the mixed bed is exhausted it is backwashed by by forcing water in the reverse upward direction. The lighter anion resins gets displaced on top and the heavier cation resins remain at the bottom. Then regenerate anion resin beads with NAOH and cation beads with Sulphuric acid. <br />\n<br />\nAMBERLITE marketed by Rohm and Haas is usually used on chemical tankers as they are available in  major ports. <br />\n<br />\nAmberlite MB20---- Ionically equilibrated mixed bed resin. Mixture of strongly acidic cation exchanger with a strongly basic type anion exchanger.($)<br />\n<br />\nAmberlite UP6150---  Fully regenerated mixed bed of cation and anion exchange resins.($$)<br />\n<br />\nAmberlite IRN150---  Gelular polystyrene cation and anion exchange resin ($$$--expensive)<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nWater softening is done by cation exchange using Alumino silicate gel. <br />\n<br />\nDe ionizing and demineralising involves two steps. Soluble salts are converted to acids by passing through a Hydrogen exchanger. Secondly they are removed by an acid adsorbent or synthetic resin. <br />\n<br />\nMineral contaminants are usually present in ionized form.<br />\n<br />\nIn general cation resin for water softening and demineralization may last 5 to 10 years. Anion resins used in demineralization last anywhere from 3 to 5 years and are dependent on operational conditions. Like every other resin, the life of mixed bed resin is dependent on the application in which it is being used. <br />\n<br />\nResin life is difficult to predict; in critical applications it\u2019s best to start analyzing and benchmarking the resin at least once per year.<br />\n<br />\nFew terms:--<br />\nExchange capacity: This is the weight of ions that can be retained per unit volume ( or sometime per unit weight ) of the exchange material concerned<br />\n<br />\nBed volume: volume per hours of liquid to be treated / volume of resin<br />\n<br />\nIon flux: Bed volume * salinity of water<br />\n<br />\nRegeneration level: weight of reagent used / volume of ion exchange material <br />\n<br />\nRegeneration rate: 100* (grams-equivalents of regenerating reagent)/ (grams-equivalents of the eluted ions)<br />\n<br />\nRegeneration efficiency: This is the opposite ratio above<br />\n<br />\nIon leakage: This is the concentration of unwanted ion left in the treated liquid<br />\n<br />\nIn European ports it is cheaper to get a truck of DI water which is wasted from nuclear plants.<br />\n<br />\nUse Graco pumps ( President and Monark models ) for spraying DI water.<br />\n<br />\nFor the uninitiated after reading the above---<br />\n<br />\nCheck the taste of the DI water you generate before spraying it on a zinc bulkhead\u2014 if the taste is acidic sour , check the pH. As you already know zinc silicate lining can take only 6 to 9 pH.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nSINGLE FILTER DEMINERALISER.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nThe practical aspects of a common place DI water single cylinder mixed bed filter , available on board Che,ical tankers is described herein.<br />\n<br />\nThe cylinder is mounted vertically and has a working pressure of 8 bars. The max pressure should be 2 bars higher. Install a pressure relief valve in your system if there is no effective control of max line pressure.<br />\n<br />\nThe mixed bed resin used here is a polishing resin, to produce ultra pure water from FWG water feed. Don\u2019t try to use shore water as you will exhaust the resin fast. You can measure the out put by chloride PPM or by using a conductivity meter\u2014the max allowed is  750 uS/ cm<br />\n<br />\nPureness of the DI water depends on flow velocity through filter. Ensure the water flows in the correct direction. After filling the mixed bed resin, fill the water slowly at first.<br />\n<br />\nAfter use the bed must be dry after draining out all water. Filter capacity for this model is about 250 to 900 litres per hour<br />\n<br />\nReplace the resin when the conductivity becomes high eg- 10 uS/cm or in case the resin if it has a coloring agent, gets discoloured.<br />\n<br />\nYou can regenerate the exhausted resin, if you land it ashore. To remove old resin put the filter horizontal and flush out with water.<br />\n<br />\nREFILLING RESIN:---<br />\n<br />\nTake the riser pipe with bottom distributor out of the filter.<br />\nClose the top end of the riser pipe with some tape<br />\nMake sure that the riser pipe and the bottom distributor is not filled with resin. Put the riser pipe with bottom distributor into the filter<br />\nPut funnel on top of the filter and fill the resin<br />\nTake care during filling that the riser pipe is situated in the middle of the filling hole<br />\nAfter filling , take the funnel off<br />\nTake the tape off the riser pipe.<br />\nClean the internal thread of the filter carefully.<br />\nClean the top distributor and mount it on the adaptor<br />\nMount this assembly on the riser pipe and filter.<br />\nScrew the adaptor clockwise hand tight<br />\nConnect the FW inlet and outlet pipes<br />\nFilter is now ready for use. Water enters from top and exits from below.<br />\n<br />\nProforma: Conductivity / PPM chlorides/ Production in tons<br />\n<br />\n1 / 0.3 /  750 <br />\n2 / 0.6 /  375<br />\n5 / 1.5 /  150<br />\n10 / 3 /  75<br />\n20 / 6 /  37<br />\n<br />\nIn case the conductivity is above the desired limits , reduce the flow through the filter. If this does not give results, renew the resin.  You can convert conductivity into ppm , by using a graph provided.<br />\n<br />\nFor best results the filter must be properly installed and operated as per the instruction manual.<br />\n<br />\nAfter the end of DM water production, if the filter will not be used for a period longer than one week, drain all water from the filer, leaving it dry. Close both inlet and outlet valves.<br />\n<br />\nProtect the system and the resin from frost. No make of resin in the filter can stand frost.<br />\n<br />\nMaintain a log, with columns for date, FW quality from FWG in pp, flow rate in litres/ hour, DI water out put ppm and DI water quality in litres.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-QEEJg-TYqH8/XIzwIe9JTpI/AAAAAAABgLg/BfmdoaqoZkkZDexNMp-k2yyknChiJqVLACLcBGAs/s1600/water-wwsoftening-ion-exchange-process.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" data-original-height=\"279\" data-original-width=\"471\" height=\"378\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-QEEJg-TYqH8/XIzwIe9JTpI/AAAAAAABgLg/BfmdoaqoZkkZDexNMp-k2yyknChiJqVLACLcBGAs/s640/water-wwsoftening-ion-exchange-process.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nWATER HARDNESS is defined as concentration of Cal/ Mag cations in terms of Calcium Carbonate.  Concentration is measured in degrees hardness. There are many units like American/ English/ French/ German hardness etc.<br />\n<br />\nHardness units: 1 ppm = 1 mg/l = 0.1 Fr = 0.07 Cl = 0.02 Meq/l<br />\n<br />\nFr = French   Cl = Clarke   Meq = milli equivalent<br />\n<br />\nGood fresh water has a hardness of 2  while seawater has a hardness of 6800 mg/l<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-CGeEVZHroBM/XIzxBxDTQRI/AAAAAAABgL0/HM0CllrgENk2f6IimHXQKNAcY2IG4uzbACLcBGAs/s1600/Water%252Bsoftening%252Bis%252Bthe%252Bremoval%252Bof%252Bcalcium%252C%252Bmagnesiumhh%252C%252Band%252Bcertain%252Bother%252Bmetal%252Bcations%252Bin%252Bhard%252Bwater.%252BThe%252Bresulting%252Bsoft%252Bwater%252Bis%252Bmore%252Bcompatible%252Bwith%252Bsoap%252Band%252Bextends%252Bthe%252Blifetime%252Bof%252Bplumbing.%252BWater%252Bsoftening%252Bis%252Busual.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "8", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/8083689494400841863/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "5161357249120978860", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-04-28T00:03:00+05:30", "updated": "2012-11-06T09:49:08+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzUyMTc1NTQ4MTA5Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/04/radha-binod-pal-forgotten-indian-capt.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/5161357249120978860", "title": "RADHA BINOD PAL, THE FORGOTTEN INDIAN--   CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S9cxoP8BcLI/AAAAAAAAAJY/Q0GXAYoIVTg/s1600/Hideki-Tojo_1607921c+(1).jpg\"><img alt=\"\" border=\"0\" id=\"BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5464891240380199090\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S9cxoP8BcLI/AAAAAAAAAJY/Q0GXAYoIVTg/s1600/Hideki-Tojo_1607921c+(1).jpg\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0px 10px 10px 0px;\" /></a><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S9cu0dkiIVI/AAAAAAAAAJQ/tBefjPdT7gE/s1600/Radha_Binod_Pal_Yasukuni_112135010_24372cdf47_o.jpg\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img alt=\"\" border=\"0\" id=\"BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5464888151663321426\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S9cu0dkiIVI/AAAAAAAAAJQ/tBefjPdT7gE/s1600/Radha_Binod_Pal_Yasukuni_112135010_24372cdf47_o.jpg\" style=\"float: left; margin: 0px 10px 10px 0px; text-align: center;\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<b><span style=\"font-size: large;\">RADHA BINOD PAL \u2013 VICTORS JUSTICE-- WAR CRIME TRIBUNAL- &nbsp;HIDEKI TOJO HAIKU- HIROSHIMA NAGASAKI </span></b><br />\n<br />\nA few years ago I stayed in Japan for a month to take delivery of a new ship , from the yard.  <br />\n<br />\nDuring one of the official dinners , the boss of the yard asked me if I knew PERRUYYA.  I was taken aback a bit, still I said yes.<br />\n<br />\nAnd then the man shed a few tears , and then continued on and on about Perruya\u2014 what a great hero he is for the Japanese people, and how his shrine at Chiyoda Tokyo is a place of worhip. <br />\n<br />\nMy puzzled Canadian Chief Engineer asked me,  \u201c Who the hell is this guy? \u201c.   <br />\n<br />\nI said \u201c He means Pal Lawyer!,  I\u2019ll tell you later, about him  \u201d <br />\n<br />\nMy chief engineer whispered into my ear \u201c How can Perruyya be Pal Lawyer? \u201c . <br />\n<br />\nI said \u201c When one of my officers Japanese girl friends got upset with my second officer for ditching her , she had barged into the officers lounge and shouted  \u201c I don\u2019t rrike you, I don\u2019t rrove you, you are butter frry,  you are prray boy,  you are ARRU FUCKIN\u2019 BARRU \u201c . This could only have meant - \u201c You are a butterfly, you are a playboy , you are all balls !\u201d <br />\n<br />\n--considering Japs can\u2019t pronounce L , like how the Chinks can\u2019t pronounce R.<br />\n<br />\nIn Rabaul ( Papua New Guinea ) I have seen from my cabin port hole , Japanese tourists lying face down on the mud on top of one of the World war 11 Japanese warship wrecks \u2013 I knew how emotional they could get over their dead ancestors.<br />\n<br />\nRadha Binod Pal (27 January 1886 \u2013 10 January 1967) was just one of the 11 jurists of the International military tribunal set up after the 2nd word war, known as Tokyo trials, to punish the Japanese . <br />\n<br />\nOnly one person was a career judge \u2013 the ex-professor of Law at Calcutta University, Justice Radhabinod Pal. The rest, mostly British, American and Australian were either ex-army officers or diplomats.  Except for Judge Radhabinod Pal, no one had any legal training, formal or informal. No wonder Pal was the most eloquent and informed man on the bench in matters of international law . <br />\n<br />\nPal was expected to toe the line of his white ex-masters. However Pal had the courage to stand by his convictions. He refused to let Allied political concerns and purposes, let alone the charter, influence his judgment in any way . While clearly acknowledging the fact that the Japanese were indeed guilty of horrendous war crimes, he argued that the Allies who were judging them were also guilty of the same. <br />\n<br />\nIndeed he questioned the very legitimacy of the Military Tribunal, and argued that it was driven solely by the spirit of retribution rather than international law. According to his view, the trial was the judgment of the vanquished by the victors; such proceedings, even if clothed in the garb of law, resulted in nothing but the satisfaction of the desire for vengeance. <br />\n<br />\nIn his lone dissent, he refers to the trial as a \"sham employment of legal process for the satisfaction of a thirst for revenge.\" His very detailed document of dissent was promptly banned from publication, for many years. His judgement that the Allies were also equally guilty of war crimes, and that victors justice cannot be endorsed , was not palatable , at all.  <br />\n<br />\nHe brought in Hiroshima and Nagasaki in his judgment as atrocities comparable with Nazi crimes. No wonder Justice Radhabinod Pal has the status of a national hero in Japan. <br />\n<br />\nA memorial in his honor is prominent in the Yasukuni shrine in Tokyo. <br />\n<br />\nIn 1966, the Emperor of Japan conferred upon Pal the First Class of the Order of the Sacred Treasure when he visited Japan. He remarked that  he had admired Japan from a young age for being the only Asian nation that \"stood up against the West.\"<br />\n<br />\nWhen Japanese Prime minister Shinzo Abe visited India ,in August 2007 he remember how Pal had saved his grandfather Nobusuke Kishi, guilty of war crimes, and the Japanese Emperor, from the gallows. (Japanese Prime Minister Hideki Tojo , who sanctioned the attack on Pearl Harbour, was however hanged . Hideki Tojo left a haiku written in Pal's honour before going to the gallows) .  <br />\n<br />\nPal would bow to the Japanese benches every time he entered the court, irritating all. This was despite , that the number of Indian combatants killed in World War II exceeded the numbers of those of most of the other countries directly involved.&nbsp; And Indians soldiers of Subash Chandra Bose's INA were tricked into digging 650 kilometers of tunnels in Rabaul-- a task worse than death itself. &nbsp;And all of them were eaten for food--except for a few who escaped into the dense jungles..<br />\n<br />\nPrime Minister Shinzo Abe met with Pal's son, Prasanta, in Kolkata . They chatted for half an hour at a city hotel.<br />\n<br />\nPal is also worshipped at the Kao Kannon temple at Atami. The ashes of Hideki Tojo is preserved here.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://3.gvt0.com/vi/-oBfWS6BEPs/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/-oBfWS6BEPs&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/-oBfWS6BEPs&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://0.gvt0.com/vi/N9wulkyMbNQ/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/N9wulkyMbNQ&fs=1&source=uds\" /><param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" /><embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/N9wulkyMbNQ&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-w_7ENd68FtQ/Ti6smlh9zzI/AAAAAAAAEhU/jmeyn_8YnLI/s1600/octopussy.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"320\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-w_7ENd68FtQ/Ti6smlh9zzI/AAAAAAAAEhU/jmeyn_8YnLI/s320/octopussy.JPG\" width=\"206\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<br />\n<br />\nCAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n..</div>\n", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "13", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/5161357249120978860/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "4559236803346367122", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-04-24T02:20:00+05:30", "updated": "2012-06-14T22:36:52+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzM5NjkzNjEyOTc2Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/04/rape-of-subconscious-mind-capt-ajit.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/4559236803346367122", "title": "THE RAPE OF THE SUBCONSCIOUS MIND -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S9IJfjPqm-I/AAAAAAAAADQ/MZxi1SKCb9s/s1600/images.jpg\"><img alt=\"\" border=\"0\" id=\"BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5463439735595375586\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S9IJfjPqm-I/AAAAAAAAADQ/MZxi1SKCb9s/s320/images.jpg\" style=\"cursor: pointer; float: left; height: 122px; margin: 0px 10px 10px 0px; width: 122px;\" /></a><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nTHE RAPE OF THE SUBCONSCIOUS \u2013 -- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n<br />\nArnold Swartznegger was given a truth serum in the Hollywood movie \u201c True Lies \u201c. <br />\n<br />\nAll of a sudden it became fashionable to use truth serum to force criminal suspects to tell the truth..<br />\n<br />\nRecently I saw the method of using narcoanalysis (Sodium Pentothal) on the so called killers of a school girl by the name of Aarushi Talwar, on a Indian national TV channel.<br />\n<br /><em>Note:- I am a bit of a body language expert.&nbsp;&nbsp; I do NOT see any real embedded grief in her own parents -- whose flesh and blood she is.</em>&nbsp; <em>Where is the catch?</em><br />\n<br />\nI hasten to say, I found the method of interrogation 100% wrong. I was surprised that no experts objected, during the subsequent days . <br />\n<br />\nThese interrogators had no dang idea how the human subconscious works. During narcoanalysis , you must NOT suggest to the patient, like a hypnotist. The patient may own up for a murder he has never done. Hypnosis is a whole different ball game.<br />\n<br />\nNo justice was being done to the poor men ( scape goats actually ) being interrogated, who were getting slapped regularly to prevent them from falling asleep.<br />\n<br />\nSubconscious mind responds to stimuli not pressure. A truth serum must not be used to weaken the resolve of the subject and make him more compliant to pressure. <br />\n<br />\nIt is a crime to RAPE the subconscious mind , by ignorant misuse of truth serum sodium pentathol . <br />\n<br />\nBy injecting a truth serum a subject's delusions, fears and fantasies cannot be distinguished from reality. People would even confess to crimes that they clearly did not commit, perhaps the murder of a non-existent mistress or rape of his neighbour. <br />\n<br />\nBrain is not capable of distinguishing between reality and memory\u2014the same neurons are sparked when we see something as when we merely remember it. <br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO8s6pt7HRI/AAAAAAAAAxY/2ytNZHs9zik/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" ox=\"true\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TO8s6pt7HRI/AAAAAAAAAxY/2ytNZHs9zik/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nBrain cannot distinguish between an image of experience and one of vivid imagination. You can participate in an orgy or think of an orgy, your wee willie winkie will give the same standing ovation.<br />\n<br />\nThis drug, Sodium Pentothal is usually used in medicine as sedatives. It acts as a depressant on the central nervous system and bring on a state of complete relaxation and a feeling of well-being. It just makes you chatty, as inhibitions are lost.. <br />\n<br />\nSo all that a \"truth serum\" will do is probably loosen a person's tongue when you're very suggestible during the sedative, or relaxed, stage of anaesthesia. But there's absolutely no guarantee of truth. <br />\n<br />\nThe reality is that you stay in this stage for only a very short time - so you have to be continually \"topped up\" with more drugs. This can involve many injections ( probably half a dozen) over a period of 2 - 8 hours. Sometimes with improper dose , the subject does not increase truth-telling, but merely increases talking; hence, both truth and bull will be revealed in that construct. The patient may lose the inhibition, but may not lose his self-control. . There is no drug that will relax a person's defences so that they will happily and reliably reveal the truth, the whole truth, and nothing but the truth.<br />\n<br />\nThe only 100% reliable way is to falsely give the subject the tendency to believe that he has revealed more than they actually did, and then make him confess the next day , at a time when his system is totally free of this drug\u2014 basically a form of trickery.<br />\n<br />\nIf you were to drink a glass of water with Sodium Pentothal, it would depress your central nervous system, slow your heart rate and lower your blood pressure. All of the listed above affects are the functions of any commonplace sedative.<br />\n<br />\nWhen a person is in coma , anastesia, narco serum, shock, seizure or sleeping\u2014the subconscious minds are wide open. Anything that will be said in their presence will be accepted by the spirit which will begin carrying it out. <br />\n<br />\nAny passing comment or trivial statements can have a devastating effect on our subconscious mind because it is not argumentative or analytical. It accepts all statements directly on the face value. Even prayers and beliefs are positive signals which we give to our subconscious mind as something acceptable and true.<br />\n<br />\nThe subconscious mind cannot tell the difference between a real experience and one that you vividly imagine. , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">ENCYCLOPEDIAS DID NOT\nRECORD IT, TILL THIS BLOGSITE FORCED THEM TO&nbsp;\n.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">THIS 90 MILLION DOES\nNOT INCLUDE THE FAMINE DEATHS&nbsp; IN INDIA\n\u2013DELIBERATELY INTRODUCED IN SUCH A FERTILE COUNTRY..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"background-color: cyan;\">9.8 million\n</span>Indians&nbsp; died in the great DELIBERATE\nfamine of 1769- -deliberately starved by Rothschild controlled East India company\nemployee Warren Hastings , who wanted Opium , Indigo and Jute for export\ninstead of food.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Nobody talks about the\ngreat DELIBERATE Guntur famine in 1832 to make people lose hope and force them\nto migrate as Indentured labour in foreign lands .&nbsp; <span style=\"background-color: yellow;\">Rothschild planned two years in advance as in\n1834 Black slavery was abolished and replaced by Indian Indentured labour.</span><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Nobody talks about the\ngreat DELIBERATE Orissa famine caused by Rothschild in 1866 / 67 where <span style=\"background-color: cyan;\">5.8\nmillion </span>Indians died of starvation .There was mass exodus and indentured labour\nto foreign lands<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">Nobody talks about the\ngreat DELIBERATE famine in India of 1876\u201378 where <span style=\"background-color: cyan;\">6.3 million</span> Indians died ,\nwhile 61 million Indians starved . Again there was mass exodus to foreign lands\nas indentured labour.<o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-size: large;\">We Indians are more\nfamiliar with the DELIBERATE famine in 1943 ( Bengal ) for which Amartya sen\ngot the Nobel prize when <span style=\"background-color: cyan;\">5.2 million</span> Indians died. &nbsp; Rothschild screwed the Bengali clan of\nSubhash Chandra Bose who dared to jump from British camp to Jap camp in the\nmiddle of WW2</span><span style=\"font-size: 12pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\"><em>Some push us around, some curse us</em></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\"><em>Where is our splendor and prestige ?</em></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\"><em>Why is there no respect for us in this world?</em></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">--  200 year old Indian immigrant song</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-PD8ebNdzFMo/TWg-qRFcM2I/AAAAAAAADrs/6EED4aX94O8/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-PD8ebNdzFMo/TWg-qRFcM2I/AAAAAAAADrs/6EED4aX94O8/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">My first introduction to indentured labour was in 1975 when as a young third officer my ship was navigating off Suriname. I had the DF on MW and heard Hindi and Bhojpuri mix with a strange accent on radio . </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-FFcUDMQKbKM/Uy68GRX3gdI/AAAAAAAAqrs/uMwUbb59it0/s1600/Jamaica_titihumb%5B2%5D.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"275\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-FFcUDMQKbKM/Uy68GRX3gdI/AAAAAAAAqrs/uMwUbb59it0/s1600/Jamaica_titihumb%5B2%5D.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Seeing my puzzled look, my old quarter master told me that half the population of Suriname are the descendants of Indentured labor from India . He told me a few shocking stories narrated to him when he was a young strapping sailor by Lascars.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Bi1XouJcgKo/Uy677ZnuAaI/AAAAAAAAqrk/d-5Iqxsk0og/s1600/SA1_thum76iob%5B4%5D.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"266\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-Bi1XouJcgKo/Uy677ZnuAaI/AAAAAAAAqrk/d-5Iqxsk0og/s1600/SA1_thum76iob%5B4%5D.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Now lascar is also a derogatory term like coolie\u2014only difference being Lascar is  Indian sailor scum who worked under European officers on olden sailing tall ships.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-2PkqZ7Ttq6U/TWg_DtEjIQI/AAAAAAAADr0/Zyo2ggONklM/s1600/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"265\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-2PkqZ7Ttq6U/TWg_DtEjIQI/AAAAAAAADr0/Zyo2ggONklM/s320/images+%25284%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Since then whenever my ship went to lands where Indian indentured labour worked two centuries ago , I made it a point to get information .  Countries like Guyana, Suriname, Trinidad, Jamaica, South Africa, Mauritius, Fiji, Reunion , Kenya , Tanzania, Malaya etc had the bulk of Indian labour.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPSBpKYVOeI/AAAAAAAABKE/Fdk6zalPVSA/s1600/images+%252844%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"280\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPSBpKYVOeI/AAAAAAAABKE/Fdk6zalPVSA/s400/images+%252844%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Most of the time it would be Government servants of Indian origin like Immigration, Customs, port Health, agents etc who visited the ship for arrival formalities. The young lot only knew that they were Indians , almost all of them used Bollywood movies to be in touch with their roots. </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LrhPrsZPZoU/TWg_GzmWvBI/AAAAAAAADr4/Y7YeY5Ela8Q/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"336\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-LrhPrsZPZoU/TWg_GzmWvBI/AAAAAAAADr4/Y7YeY5Ela8Q/s640/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">These countries have destroyed all history of indentured labour , even in their history text books of school.  The idea was to destroy their psyche and to destroy the fountainhead of spirit.. I had specific questions for them about their wretched history and they would come back and tell after consulting their nostalgic grandparents.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cdSC7cjCI3w/Uy67j-jC3eI/AAAAAAAAqrc/xc5mH8VWbYY/s1600/M2_thumb%5B11869%5D.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"258\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-cdSC7cjCI3w/Uy67j-jC3eI/AAAAAAAAqrc/xc5mH8VWbYY/s1600/M2_thumb%5B11869%5D.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Such interaction invariably rekindled something inside their DNA and they hoped to visit India to trace their roots and culture. All of them were happy and privileged to speak to an original Indian from the motherland.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hZryjS9tK24/TiaSmEwnXII/AAAAAAAAEJs/i9uy-dhaa1Y/s1600/imagesCAW10GV2.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"640\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-hZryjS9tK24/TiaSmEwnXII/AAAAAAAAEJs/i9uy-dhaa1Y/s640/imagesCAW10GV2.jpg\" width=\"497\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Around 1834 the English speaking white man abolished slavery.  He then reinvented slavery in the form of Indentured labour from India. It was a worse form of slavery. Attractive ,glowing , blushing , dark skinned young Indian women , now came into the equation.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR88o6mhfI/AAAAAAAABJg/5YnO9JLJZMs/s1600/images+%252835%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR88o6mhfI/AAAAAAAABJg/5YnO9JLJZMs/s1600/images+%252835%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR9B4ya5aI/AAAAAAAABJk/dsQUdKU-4uM/s1600/images+%252834%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR9B4ya5aI/AAAAAAAABJk/dsQUdKU-4uM/s1600/images+%252834%2529.jpg\" width=\"265\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It was a win-win situation for the sailors on ships on the long 20 week voyage and the white colonial masters and overseers in the destination country.  After all the black slave women could not hold their interest.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR-wAOrn5I/AAAAAAAABJw/RL8CqPBQfk8/s1600/images+%252838%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"266\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR-wAOrn5I/AAAAAAAABJw/RL8CqPBQfk8/s1600/images+%252838%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR_U7vXtgI/AAAAAAAABJ0/qI-SnCpnr_g/s1600/images+%252839%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"264\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR_U7vXtgI/AAAAAAAABJ0/qI-SnCpnr_g/s1600/images+%252839%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Recruiting agents in India called Arkatia ( the hook ) were paid a handsome some for good looking native women. Invariably the naive protector husbands, fathers or brothers of such women would mysteriously fall overboard, get killed or get missing.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;These gullible males used to be promised cushy supervisory jobs and handsome wages and the promise that the promised land is just over the horizon. Some women were just kidnapped and shanghaied. Some were child widows who had nothing to lose. </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR9eq_FtEI/AAAAAAAABJo/AowYXQl_sxI/s1600/images+%252837%2529.jpg\" /></a></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPSAPtaQvPI/AAAAAAAABJ4/OVwKe2En_lI/s1600/images+%252841%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"231\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPSAPtaQvPI/AAAAAAAABJ4/OVwKe2En_lI/s400/images+%252841%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPSATf4d50I/AAAAAAAABJ8/kJXkEhOOLC8/s1600/images+%252840%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"231\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPSATf4d50I/AAAAAAAABJ8/kJXkEhOOLC8/s400/images+%252840%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">All were duped into signing ( thumb printing ) extensive 5 year contracts with vague terms and conditions in English, which they could not understand. The British government in India and even the Christian missionaries did nothing to stop this blatant mass deception. Sometimes just before sailing women would be secretly  separated from their husbands and put on the next ship. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-l8A_gtb9GeI/TiaTSsffsvI/AAAAAAAAEJ0/nxGoP1sSqi0/s1600/imagesCAUO66R8.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-l8A_gtb9GeI/TiaTSsffsvI/AAAAAAAAEJ0/nxGoP1sSqi0/s1600/imagesCAUO66R8.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A lot of women died of venereal diseases. A lot men and children died on the sea passage due to dysentery, typhoid, malnutrition etc. The ships doctor would be given a bonus for every person delivered alive. </span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/--Tdh63Cg3Bg/TmTM9ocDkXI/AAAAAAAAF_8/Q-7a5SMGoHY/s1600/imagesCAE5IC2F.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"266\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/--Tdh63Cg3Bg/TmTM9ocDkXI/AAAAAAAAF_8/Q-7a5SMGoHY/s400/imagesCAE5IC2F.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The survivors of the terrible sea voyage kala paani ordeal, sitting , sleeping and eating amidst their own waste,  identified themselves with the ship they travelled and forged a sense of unity and strong bhai\u2014behen bonds, with only their religion , culture and festivals for spiritual resilience and support.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR9kNJDO5I/AAAAAAAABJs/LIbfzk-EO0Q/s1600/images+%252836%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"301\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR9kNJDO5I/AAAAAAAABJs/LIbfzk-EO0Q/s400/images+%252836%2529.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR8Jerd2fI/AAAAAAAABJc/A4rrITBCPP8/s1600/images+%252832%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR8Jerd2fI/AAAAAAAABJc/A4rrITBCPP8/s1600/images+%252832%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">More than a million Indentured Indians landed in the Caribbean itself. A lot of them were cotton and Indigo workers whose industries were destroyed by the British East India company (owned by Rothschild German Jews).&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-MmQAdzJ4blo/UyagPGQk5zI/AAAAAAAAqaQ/IVn_3bZMnVA/s1600/62jetk5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"424\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-MmQAdzJ4blo/UyagPGQk5zI/AAAAAAAAqaQ/IVn_3bZMnVA/s1600/62jetk5.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Prime fertile land was earmarked for growing opium, to be sold in China for massive profits.&nbsp; An onerous taxation system forced many starving farmers off their land. Vague records were maintained. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-w0TjJ075GSg/TmTM2bvjWZI/AAAAAAAAF_4/bmXrlLcV5eY/s1600/imagesCAKZQS1U.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"384\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-w0TjJ075GSg/TmTM2bvjWZI/AAAAAAAAF_4/bmXrlLcV5eY/s640/imagesCAKZQS1U.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Most of the indentured labour were from UP, Bihar, Orissa, Bengal and Tamil nadu.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR7wM4ua1I/AAAAAAAABJQ/J_NB-ieVoco/s1600/images+%252828%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR7wM4ua1I/AAAAAAAABJQ/J_NB-ieVoco/s1600/images+%252828%2529.jpg\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">As soon as the Indentured Indian landed ashore he would be marched to estates and housed in slave barracks without mattresses or pillows.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7QKOjiSPdN4/Uyaen03v7MI/AAAAAAAAqZI/_mEzSek7Qq0/s1600/v0ktddt277.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"282\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-7QKOjiSPdN4/Uyaen03v7MI/AAAAAAAAqZI/_mEzSek7Qq0/s1600/v0ktddt277.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Life was dehumanizing, with no honour, little pay, poor diet, long toiling hours , insults , monetary fines and floggings with cattle whips at the slightest provocation. </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-GYN-qfOVdhQ/TiaSxnMcZEI/AAAAAAAAEJw/HiIL7cabENY/s1600/imagesCAEPTQ80.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-GYN-qfOVdhQ/TiaSxnMcZEI/AAAAAAAAEJw/HiIL7cabENY/s1600/imagesCAEPTQ80.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Cat of nine tails was used on deserters to bloody their backs and then rubbed with chillie and salt. Most of the time these \"deserters\" were the guys who objected to their pretty wives and sisters being taken away by the white man to his home for sex.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-HYJ--snETrk/TWg-wydOPeI/AAAAAAAADrw/uX6oZpDCiY8/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-HYJ--snETrk/TWg-wydOPeI/AAAAAAAADrw/uX6oZpDCiY8/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Death from Malaria, Typhoid, TB , Cholera , Beriberi, Hookworm etc took the toll. There was no clean water or latrines. They were unable even to bury or cremate the dead. In Grenada about 2000 sick Indians were kicked off the estate to die on the road side, nude ,skeleton ed and maggotted with even the parish missionaries turning the other way from these poor wailing souls . </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/--LUkkBGoQ4w/TmTMpwU_qRI/AAAAAAAAF_0/KyFPlPw-2Z4/s1600/imagesCA27XPIG.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/--LUkkBGoQ4w/TmTMpwU_qRI/AAAAAAAAF_0/KyFPlPw-2Z4/s1600/imagesCA27XPIG.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">In Africa while building rail and roads they were eaten up by lions . After completing their 5 year contract they had to pay for their return fare. </span><br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">And with monetary fines for small offences, there was little money.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR7zvuo1EI/AAAAAAAABJU/1R4CIXPnU2w/s1600/images+%252829%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TPR7zvuo1EI/AAAAAAAABJU/1R4CIXPnU2w/s1600/images+%252829%2529.jpg\" width=\"307\" /></span></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A new born child would be arbitrarily recorded as \u201c coolie\u201d with name of father and mother also as \u201ccoolie \u201c.  If you go to South Africa , where there are currently about 1.2 million Indians--and look into the telephone directory there are more NAIDOOS than the Naidus in India.  </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IhyJW_LQalo/TmTMcXiRrOI/AAAAAAAAF_w/VjYR1a_o4zM/s1600/imagesCAT2J2X8.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"363\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-IhyJW_LQalo/TmTMcXiRrOI/AAAAAAAAF_w/VjYR1a_o4zM/s640/imagesCAT2J2X8.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The grapevine is as follows \u2014 a ship lands up , the white immigration officer is drunk, hot  and bothered seeing so many monkey look alikes .  He says \u201c All of you fuc#ers are NAIDOOS \u2014 carry on!\u201d . </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Seychelles&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;9,000<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Others &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;47,000<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The majority of the Indians living\nin the English-speaking Caribbean came from eastern Uttar Pradesh and western\nBihar, while those brought to Guadeloupe and Martinique were mostly from, &nbsp;from Andhra Pradesh and Tamil Nadu. About\ntwenty two percent of the indentured were Tamils and Telugus particularly in\nTrinidad and Tobago, and Guyana.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-SBGKdvBIBG0/Uy66N24mBsI/AAAAAAAAqrU/nWB6Uz5XzS4/s1600/indentured+servaney4yhet+advertisement.gif\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em;
