text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-toM9t4Lhew0/TmTMLXne6ZI/AAAAAAAAF_o/R1ofIo7ABls/s1600/imagesCAUEHPK3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"377\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/-toM9t4Lhew0/TmTMLXne6ZI/AAAAAAAAF_o/R1ofIo7ABls/s400/imagesCAUEHPK3.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Fabulously rich John Gladstone, (1763-1851) owned almost all the sugar plantations in Jamaica, and was the biggest slave trader .&nbsp; He was the stooge of Opium runner and British East India company owner, German Jew R0thschild, &nbsp;in British Parliament, where he was MP for 9 years.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-GbbPr2IHlr4/UyafU5zQj5I/AAAAAAAAqZo/HrfJH6sOyFQ/s1600/ima67eoges.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"358\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-GbbPr2IHlr4/UyafU5zQj5I/AAAAAAAAqZo/HrfJH6sOyFQ/s1600/ima67eoges.jpg\" width=\"640\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">When slavery was abolished he was desperate to get Indentured labour from India, in his estates. The Indians lived in worse slave like conditions, and he would NOT even feed them properly.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xB4BuCvdUss/TWg9PHizUyI/AAAAAAAADro/u5eClgL7pGE/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"234\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-xB4BuCvdUss/TWg9PHizUyI/AAAAAAAADro/u5eClgL7pGE/s1600/images+%252811%2529.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This evil and greedy man fooled the Indians by false promises. From 1838 to 1917, In British Guiana alone 260, 000 Indians were slaves. He bribed British Prime minister Sir Robert Peel, and made himself a Baronet in 1846. Then he bribed again using his Rothschild connection, and made sure his son , William Ewart Gladstone, was in politics in the cabinet of \"good friend\" Robert Peel, and in line to be future Prime Minister of UK.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-A5E3H2IvGvA/UyagE9RoZNI/AAAAAAAAqaI/ywV39325H08/s1600/imatk+yfges.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"268\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-A5E3H2IvGvA/UyagE9RoZNI/AAAAAAAAqaI/ywV39325H08/s1600/imatk+yfges.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">AN APOLOGY IS LONG OVERDUE.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">I have interviewed lot\nof Telugu Indians aboard who were Indentured slaves- a lot of them in South Africa\u2014the\nNAIDOOOS, the GOVENDERS , the PATIYAACHIS, the MOODLEYS &nbsp;. I went to their homes and talked to their\ngrandfathers.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Some remember as\nTERRIBLE GUNTUR FAMINE in 1832. &nbsp;&nbsp;They said there was NO cholera or small pox\u2014it\nwas DELIBERATE famine created by the white invader to make them lose hope, convert them to indentured coolies.. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Most of the Guntur ,\nMasulipatnam (Machilipatnam) Indians were farmers and weavers. &nbsp;Masulipatnam was the the first trading\nsettlement on the East coast of India established by Rothschild for his British\nEast India Company. The famous Muslin cloth was created for the ancients Greeks\nat Masulie ( Maisolos ).&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">60% of the people of\nGuntur area when the exodis started on British East India Company ships. Sir\nWalter Elliot writes that the famine of 1833 and the following epidemic had\nprostrated Guntur district and that \"a man in perfect health was hardly to\nbe seen anywhere\".&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The superior Indian\nweaver\u2019s cloth has no buyers in Manchester and Lancaster thanks to Rothschild\ncontrolled labour unions.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The Rothschild stooge President\nof the Blackburn Chamber of Commerce said that \"the manufacturers of\nLancashire should carefully watch the doings of the Indian manufactur\u00aders, they\ndid try to place artificial obstacles in the way of development of this\nindustry in India. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The legendary Guntur\nfamine of 1832\u20131833 followed by DELIBERATE crop failure as well as excessive\nand uncertain levels of taxation on peasants. &nbsp;The ruling British East India Company took no\nmeasures were adopted to formulate any general system of famine relief or\nprevention.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Nobody talks about the great\nDELIBERATE Orissa famine deliberately caused by Rothschild in 1866 / 67 where\n5.8 million Indians died of starvation.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "93", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/1096464250714920718/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "6295444721457308933", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2010-04-10T01:23:00+05:30", "updated": "2010-12-14T15:07:22+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMjkyMzE5NDQyNzU5Cm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2010/04/passivation-on-stainless-steel-chemical.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/6295444721457308933", "title": "NITRIC AND CITRIC ACID PASSIVATION ON STAINLESS STEEL CHEMICAL TANKERS-- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S9KY99ThGVI/AAAAAAAAADo/byH1Ja3N6Ys/s1600/41272.epibrw.jpg\" onblur=\"try {parent.deselectBloggerImageGracefully();} catch(e) {}\"><img alt=\"\" border=\"0\" id=\"BLOGGER_PHOTO_ID_5463597488149698898\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/S9KY99ThGVI/AAAAAAAAADo/byH1Ja3N6Ys/s320/41272.epibrw.jpg\" style=\"cursor: hand; cursor: pointer; float: left; height: 200px; margin: 0 10px 10px 0; width: 300px;\" /></a><br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nPASSIVATION -- CITRIC VS NITRIC ACIDS-- Capt Ajit Vadakayil<br />\n<br />\nPassivation is a process to build up a layer of Chromium oxide armour on Austenetic Stainless steel of ships cargo tanks. <br />\n<br />\nThis mono-molecular oxide layer is about 10 angstroms ( one divided by 10 million-- millimeters ) is invisible , chemically unreactive, self repairing  and uni-potentialises the Stainless steel surface. The action is by oxygen and water on a clean surface.<br />\n<br />\nIt is our policy to passivate the SUS 316L and SUS 316LN austenitic SS tanks with 14% by volume cold Nitric acid . It is also our policy not to include hydrofluoric acid in a passivation solution. Hydro-flouric acid is a pickler which removes chromium and nickel along with heat hardened scale, it NOT a passivator.<br />\n<br />\nThe concentrated acid you get on board in 200 litre drums is usually 68%. Contact time for Nitric acid is 2 hours. Then rinse with Fresh water of low chlorides as obtained from ships fresh water generator tille the pH value is 7. After that allow the tank to dry by natural ventilation for about 12 hours. Before recirc acid , the tank must be totally degreased and clean of all NVM matters.<br />\n<br />\nThe usual aggressive cargoes which require passivation to de done is after dischg of wet Phosphoric acid ( fertilizer grade ) , Hot Caustic soda solution, Sulphuric acid, Epichlorohydrin etc. Prolonged washing with very hot salt water after dischg of Palm oil fatty acids etc can also cause local failure of the passive layer. Passivation is also done when free iron , rust and other NVM deposits can adversely affect the metallurgical or sanitary condition of stability of the surface.<br />\n<br />\nIn USA the Nitric acid must be carried in stainless steel drums. Sometimes the USCG has been known to give a non conformity if the Nitric acid on board is stored in Plastic drums, never mind how reputed and standard the manufacturing company is.<br />\n<br />\nWhen you read the ships Charter party find out who is going to pay for Nitric acid and for what all cargoes.   Returning empty SS drums can be a very cost intensive process. This is in addition to the rent paid for keeping the drums on board till you land it and it reaches the owners of the drum. This is not as simple or economical as returning empty bottles of oxygen and acetylene.<br />\n<br />\nThis is where passivation with Citric acid comes into the picture. It must be very clear that Citric acid passivation is only the second best. EMS wants Nitric acid passivation as far as possible. Only when the cost are excessive to the ships budget ( not charterers account ) then Citric acid passivation may be considered, provided the process is done the right way. Or if you have to load FOSFA cargoes , where you cannot declare in writing that the passivation was done with FOSFA banned Nitric acid.<br />\n<br />\nPassivating with Citric acid is a misnomer by itself, as Citric acid is not an oxidizing chemical like Nitric acid. It just removes the free iron like Nitric acid. The building up of the Chromic acid layer is now done ONLY by the magic action of oxygen and water of mother nature.  Recirc with 7% Citric acid by weight , contact time required is only one hour. Both these parameters are half that of that of Nitric acid. Rinse till pH 7 with ships FWG chloride free water But the natural venting time to get the proper angstrom thickness of CrO2 must be at least 24 hours which is double that of Nitric acid.<br />\n<br />\n############################################<br />\nPROFORMA:--- Item/   Nitric acid pure/ Citric acid formula<br />\n############################################<br />\n<br />\nStrength of acid solution to recirculate/ 14% by volume/ 7% by weight<br />\n<br />\nAcid contact time/ 2 hours/ 1 hour<br />\n<br />\nWater to use for rinsing/ FW generator water FW generator water<br />\n<br />\nRinsing till pH / 7/ 7<br />\n<br />\nSteaming tank/ No /For 30 minutes, to sweat out acid from deep pore penetrations<br />\n<br />\nVentilation/ Natural for 12 hours/ Natural for 24 hours<br />\n<br />\nChelating action ( removal of free-iron , exogeneous iron, ferrous contaminants)/ Yes/ Yes, faster<br />\n<br />\nOxidising action on SS/ Yes/ No\u2014BIG DISADVANTAGE<br />\n<br />\nFOSFA banned/ Yes/ No<br />\n<br />\nCost effective/ No/ Yes<br />\n<br />\nDegreasing required prior recirc of acid/ Yes/ Yes<br />\n<br />\nSlop retention / Changes colour (yellow)- decomposition due to sunlight/  No colour change<br />\n<br />\nToxic fumes/ Yes/ No<br />\n<br />\nPenetration into SS pittings and pores/ Good/ Very good<br />\n<br />\nFlash corrosion attack/ No/ Yes\u2014if the acid does not contain corrosion inhibitors or wetting agents<br />\n<br />\nSmog/ NOx vapours/ No<br />\n<br />\nSafe on humans/ No/ Yes<br />\n<br />\nBiodegradable/ No/ Yes<br />\n<br />\nType/ Inorganic/ Organic<br />\n<br />\nSolubility in water/ Fully soluble/ Fully soluble<br />\n<br />\nRe-use of solution/ Yes/ Longer use andlonger lasting<br />\n<br />\nAccelerators \u2013NOT TO BE USED ON OUR SHIPS--/ Sodium di chromate(oxidizer booster )in the passivation solution for faster build up of chromium oxide layer/ Very light 100 ppm solution of Hydrogen peroxide ( powerful oxidizer ) after rinsing till pH 7, to cut down the excessive ventilation time<br />\n<br />\nNegative action of recirc acid on a UN- degreased surface/ Burns grease into the<br />\npores and pittings/ Gas bubbles which affect natural passivation<br />\n<br />\nOxidisation of nickel to prevent uncontrolled tarnish/ Yes/ No<br />\n<br />\nPassivation of ordinary iron plate/ Yes/ No<br />\n<br />\nRemoval of heat hardened scale/ Yes\u2014 pickling  along with Hydroflouric acid/ No<br />\n<br />\nAS YOU CAN SEE CITRIC ACID SCORES OVER NITRIC ACID BY BEING A FASTER CHELATOR ( CHEMICAL DISSOLUTION ) , BUT HAS A HUGE DISADVANTAGE, WHICH CAN HARDLY BE WISHED AWAY OR DOWNPLAYED BY ENVIRONMENTALIST LOBBIES\u2014IT IS NOT OXIDISING REPEAT IT IS NOT OXIDISNG.  HOWEVER THE USE OF A WEAK HYDROGEN PEROXIDE SOLUTION , AS A POST PASSIVATION RINSE CAN ELIMINATE THIS PROBLEM.<br />\n<br />\nHydrogen peroxide can oxidize SS but it cannot remove free iron.  A strong solution used inadvertently can react with free iron left behind after improper chelation and affect the chromium metal.<br />\n<br />\nShips SS tanks are Austenitic in the 300 series like 316L , 316LN and 317L . What is good for  Martensitic or Ferritic grades or other series does not hold good for Austenetic grades.<br />\n<br />\nCitric acid is the same acid found in oranges and citrus fruits. It is used commonly in household cleaners and disinfectors.<br />\n<br />\nThe US EPA has recogonised the safety of Citric acid to the environment. It efficiently removes free iron from the surface of Austenetic SS and thus can be used in lesser concentrations than Nitric acid. Since it has very ,low reactivity with other metals of Austenitic SS, the slops can be retained for longer periods .<br />\n<br />\nDue to low reactivity of Citric acid with metals other than free iron it is generally safe to leave the slops on board for longer time than Nitric acid.<br />\n<br />\nWhen SS is buffed or ground with non-metallic discs, more chromium is exposed which reacts with oxygen and water to form the chromium oxide armour. If some particles of carbon steel is embedded in a rough surface then the self repairing cannot take place. Instead corrosion will take place when the metal is wetted or exposed to a corrosive environment ( galvanic couple between 2 dissimilar metals in an electrolyte ).<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc6yy1bJnI/AAAAAAAAB4w/YmUyboOfcm4/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TQc6yy1bJnI/AAAAAAAAB4w/YmUyboOfcm4/s1600/capt+ajit+vadakayil.JPG\" /></a></div><br />\n<br />\nCAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL ( 28 years of command )<br />\n..", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. font-size: large;\"><strong>ENERGY AND \u201c GOLD FINGER\u201d  TERRORISM- CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL</strong></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-u5tpk8CljxQ/T8rPCmDM9FI/AAAAAAAAL1k/NdbXc1RZKAo/s1600/imagesCA76X7R5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A few years ago my chemical tanker ship docked at Bejaya in Algeria. No shore leave was possible due to tight anti-terrorism security. ( It is from Bejaya that Fibonacci took the secrets of ZERO and Indian numerals to Europe ). A year ago some terrorists came by boat on a ship at anchorage and shot dead all the crew, for no reason.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">I had one on one conversations with few intelligent local people. They said terrorism is Algeria will stop only after all the natural gas has been bled from the country by the white man. Algeria has one of the biggest gas deposits in the world under its desert sands. </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-n_pr_hsoXgM/T8rQNvHQdjI/AAAAAAAAL2s/-kU-p1hLBQc/s1600/imagesCAWFQWF5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"264\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-n_pr_hsoXgM/T8rQNvHQdjI/AAAAAAAAL2s/-kU-p1hLBQc/s320/imagesCAWFQWF5.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; This is like trying to palm off a useless 20 year old MS DOS laptop to you , so that you will NOT buy the latest processor model .  </span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-gLzeBOn3J0U/T8rP-W0iTqI/AAAAAAAAL2c/AdLkHpsAedc/s1600/imagesCAKN6TFQ.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"239\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-gLzeBOn3J0U/T8rP-W0iTqI/AAAAAAAAL2c/AdLkHpsAedc/s320/imagesCAKN6TFQ.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Our president Abdul Kalam had told on national television years back that India must develop Thorium based nuclear reactors. Thorium contains 150 times more energy than Uranium and is the MOST efficient combustible . It is found along with actinides Uranium and Plutonium in the Periodic table. Since Thorium is only slightly radio active , it is clean with no burden of nuclear waste disposal.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-EWnGdjdmS4s/T8rP3R3iwZI/AAAAAAAAL2U/m4gqCUZ-IKw/s1600/lftr.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"291\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-EWnGdjdmS4s/T8rP3R3iwZI/AAAAAAAAL2U/m4gqCUZ-IKw/s400/lftr.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Lead derived from Thorium has higher atomic weight that lead derived from Uranium. Ordinary lead , Uranium derived lead and Thorium derived lead are physically , chemically and spectroscopically identical. Xrays which vibrate at 400000000 billion to 6000000000 times per second are chemical light phenomenon produced by Gamma rays of Uranium and Thorium.</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CIP6l3JAnIY/T8rPwSYDEBI/AAAAAAAAL2M/hE_7Mpjh1WA/s1600/LFTR_advantages.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"298\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-CIP6l3JAnIY/T8rPwSYDEBI/AAAAAAAAL2M/hE_7Mpjh1WA/s400/LFTR_advantages.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">After extraction from ore, thorium does not require energy-intensive enrichment as is the case with uranium.</span></span><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></span><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A thorium-powered reactor is inherently safe. It doesn't run the risk of \"meltdown\" or explosion nor can even a dirty bomb be created. Its nuclear reaction simply stops when its neutron exciter is turned off.</span></span><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/---OLXNxFdNA/T8rPi2Pa7lI/AAAAAAAAL2E/C29gS63i98A/s1600/Final-Thorium1.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"385\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/---OLXNxFdNA/T8rPi2Pa7lI/AAAAAAAAL2E/C29gS63i98A/s400/Final-Thorium1.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"> <span class=\"apple-style-span\">A thorium powerpack's neutron excitor does not use radioactive flux components as conventionally done for portable systems. It works of resonant phonon pair cleavage using specifically designed nuclear lattice holo-forms (holographic waveforms) to induce neutron imbalance in a host atom where the host atom then attempts to establish \"balance\" through the liberation of neutrons. </span></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qLtEN1CCNEw/T8rPbEVBBkI/AAAAAAAAL18/dEvlG3xM110/s1600/imagesCA6GHTJ9.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"299\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-qLtEN1CCNEw/T8rPbEVBBkI/AAAAAAAAL18/dEvlG3xM110/s400/imagesCA6GHTJ9.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"apple-style-span\">Commercial thorium powerpacks can be developed with 50 or 100 kilowatts of output for home use, and up to 1 megawatt for industrial use. They actually are \"power amplifiers\" with power outputs of 60 times over input power. Maintenance would be minimal.</span><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-R3vFLeo97pk/T8rPSa4-oKI/AAAAAAAAL10/W3_JTXyX268/s1600/imagesCAYEAVW5.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"298\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/-R3vFLeo97pk/T8rPSa4-oKI/AAAAAAAAL10/W3_JTXyX268/s400/imagesCAYEAVW5.jpg\" width=\"400\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><br />\n</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"></span></span><br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"apple-converted-space\">Bombardment of thorium-232 by slow neutrons yields the fissile isotope uranium-233. This process is comparable to the process by which fast neutrons \u201cbreed\u201d fissile plutonium-239 from nonfissile uranium-238.. The thorium-uranium fuel cycle is being studied by scientists as an alternative to the uranium-plutonium fuel cycle.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><br /></span></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">When you bombard the slightly\nradioactive heavy metal thorium 232 with neutrons, you convert it to\nfissionable uranium 233. Instead of water, the reactor circulates thorium\ntetrafluoride fuel through the reactor core dissolved in molten lithium and\nberyllium fluoride salts.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">A small amount of U233\u2014supplies the neutrons that\ncause fission. Excess neutrons fly off into a surrounding blanket of molten\nthorium salt to convert more thorium into new U233 fuel, which can then be used\nto keep the reaction going.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Because the molten salt expands when heated, it is\ninherently safe. The lower density fuel won't support a continuing nuclear\nreaction. Every stage of this process\u2014fuel loading, neutron management, fuel\nseparation, heat exchange, refueling, and waste separation\u2014has been\nsuccessfully tested in actual US reactors.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n</div>\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A few years ago my ship docked at Munguba inside one of the minor tributaries ( Jari )of the mighty Amazon river.
